   <h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">Annual cannabis use by country</h1> 
   <div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content"> 
    <div id="siteSub" class="noprint">
     From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia
    </div> 
    <div id="contentSub"></div> 
    <div id="contentSub2"></div> 
    <div id="jump-to-nav"></div> <a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a> <a class="mw-jump-link" href="#searchInput">Jump to search</a> 
    <div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr">
     <div class="mw-parser-output">
      <div class="shortdescription nomobile noexcerpt noprint searchaux" style="display:none">
       Wikipedia list article
      </div> 
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;">
        <a href="/wiki/File:World_map_of_countries_by_annual_prevalence_of_cannabis_use.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/64/World_map_of_countries_by_annual_prevalence_of_cannabis_use.svg/300px-World_map_of_countries_by_annual_prevalence_of_cannabis_use.svg.png" decoding="async" width="300" height="132" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/64/World_map_of_countries_by_annual_prevalence_of_cannabis_use.svg/450px-World_map_of_countries_by_annual_prevalence_of_cannabis_use.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/64/World_map_of_countries_by_annual_prevalence_of_cannabis_use.svg/600px-World_map_of_countries_by_annual_prevalence_of_cannabis_use.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="940" data-file-height="415"></a> 
        <div class="thumbcaption">

        </div>
       </div>
      </div> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       See also: <a href="/wiki/Adult_lifetime_cannabis_use_by_country" title="Adult lifetime cannabis use by country">Adult lifetime cannabis use by country</a>
      </div> 
      <p>This is a list of the annual <a href="/wiki/Prevalence" title="Prevalence">prevalence</a> of <b><a href="/wiki/Cannabis_(drug)" title="Cannabis (drug)">cannabis</a> use by country</b> (including some territories) as a percentage of the population aged 15â€“64 (unless otherwise indicated). The indicator is an "annual prevalence" rate which is the percentage of the youth and adult population who have consumed cannabis at least once in the past survey year. </p> 
      <div id="toc" class="toc" role="navigation" aria-labelledby="mw-toc-heading">
       <input type="checkbox" role="button" id="toctogglecheckbox" class="toctogglecheckbox" style="display:none">
       <div class="toctitle" lang="en" dir="ltr">

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Table">Table</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Annual_cannabis_use_by_country&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Table">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <p>The primary source of information is the <i>World Drug Report 2011</i> (WDR 2011)<sup id="cite_ref-wdr_2011_1-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-wdr_2011-1">[1]</a></sup> by the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Office_on_Drugs_and_Crime" title="United Nations Office on Drugs and Crime">United Nations Office on Drugs and Crime</a> (UNODC); some older numbers are from the <i>World Drug Report 2006</i> (WDR 2006),<sup id="cite_ref-wdr_2006_2-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-wdr_2006-2">[2]</a></sup>. </p>
